[04/04/2023, 4:33:25โฏAM] ูุญูุฏ ุงูุดููุฑู UTM: *[SURVEY OF INTERNATIONAL STUDENTS LIVING OUTSIDE OF THE CAMPUS FOR THE PURPOSE OF PROVIDING TRANSPORTATION INTO THE UTM CAMPUS]*

ุงูุณูุงู ุนูููู ูุฑุญูุฉ ุงููู ูุจุฑูุงุชู
Greetings and Hello,
ุจุณู ุงููู ุงูุฑุญูู ุงูุฑุญูู

Glad to inform that the Student Representative Council UTM is conducting a *Survey of International Students Living Outside of the Campus for the Purpose of Providing Transportation into the UTM Campus*.

This survey was made to collect data on international students living outside UTM. These data will be used to deal with problems with buses from outside to the UTM campus.

Please fill in the link below:
https://forms.gle/WsXcAojC5dGxKbeB7

It is hoped that all international students together deal with this problem.

Cooperation in this matter is greatly appreciated and is first thanked.

Thank you.

Document needed for attestation from Saudi Cultural Mission :
1. All certificate and transcript certified by Higher Education, Ministry of Foreign Affairs Malaysia and by the embassy of the country issuing the passport
2. Copy of first page of passport and all visa for the duration of study
3. A letter from the institution confirming the completion and graduation from the program and to be sent by email to attestations@my.moe.gov.sa & cultureannajwa@gmail.com
4. Original Contract certify by Saudi Chamber of commerce / letter from government entity requesting the attestation

*Fees* : Rm100 for submission cultural mission and Rm80.00 per page for Saudi Embassy
